Let's make a game!
	-Wall Destroyer Not So Real Edition
	-by Tellurium
	-created on 04/21/2014
	-last updated on 12/27/2014
	-version 3.Reaefsek

Settings :
	-prices increase by 110%
	-selling gives back 75%
	-resources are hidden by default
	-clickables are hidden by default
	-buildings are hidden by default
	-upgrades are hidden by default
	-achievements are hidden by default
	-show log
	-custom stylesheet : http://pastebin.com/raw.php?i=7zQ8tw3g
	-text color : black
	-fonts : Kavoon
	-boxes : main (resources, clickables); stats (achievements); store (upgrades, buildings)

Clickables :
	*hitWall
	-gives 1 money
	-gives 1 totalMoney
	-gives 1 handDamage
	-visible
	-named Punch wall
	-picture : http://i.imgur.com/108BtPH.png

	*makeBricks
	-gives 1 bricks
	-gives 1 totalBricks
	-gives 1 handBricks
	-named Create Bricks
	-picture : http://i.imgur.com/Tdh80P1.png

	*makeBricks2
	-gives 1 fourthWallMatter
	-gives 1 total4thWallMatter
	-gives 1 hand4thWallMatter
	-named Create 4th Wall Bricks
	-picture : http://i.imgur.com/TJGos5s.png

	*fastForward
	-gives 1 fastForwardResource
	-locks fastForward
	-unlocks disableFastForward
	-named Enable Fast Forward (x10 Production Multiplier)
	*disableFastForward
	-converts fastForwardResource to nothing
	-locks disableFastForward
	-unlocks fastForward
	-named Disable Fast Forward (Removes x10 Production Multiplier)

It's about time someone took the righteous task upon themselves of doing something about it!</i><br> <br>Destroy the wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>25</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>250,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
